+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS before_delete_chat_update_sync_chat_deletes\nBEFORE DELETE ON chat WHEN is_mic_enabled() = 1\nBEGIN\n    INSERT INTO sync_deleted_chats (guid, recordID, timestamp)\n    SELECT guid_for_chat(OLD.chat_identifier, scl.service_name, OLD.style, scl.filter_action, scl.filter_sub_action), scl.ck_record_id, m.date\n    FROM sync_chat_slice scl\n    INNER JOIN message m ON m.rowid = (\n        SELECT m.rowid FROM chat_recoverable_message_join crmj\n        INNER JOIN message m ON m.rowid = crmj.message_id\n        WHERE chat_id = scl.chat\n        ORDER BY m.date DESC\n        LIMIT 1\n    )\n    WHERE OLD.rowid = scl.chat\n    AND scl.ck_record_id IS NOT NULL;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS before_delete_chat_update_sync_chat_deletes\nBEFORE DELETE ON chat WHEN is_mic_enabled() = 1\nBEGIN\n    INSERT INTO sync_deleted_chats (guid, recordID, timestamp)\n    SELECT guid_for_chat(cpl.identifier, scps.service_name, OLD.style, scps.filter_action, scps.filter_sub_action), scps.ck_record_id, m.date\n    FROM sync_chat_part_slice scps\n    INNER JOIN chat_part cp ON scps.chat_part_id = cp.rowid\n    INNER JOIN chat_part_lookup cpl ON cpl.chat_part_id = cp.rowid AND cpl.domain = 'ChatIdentifier'\n    INNER JOIN message m ON m.rowid = (\n        SELECT m.rowid FROM chat_part_recoverable_message_join cprmj\n        INNER JOIN message m ON m.rowid = cprmj.message_id\n        WHERE cprmj.chat_part_id = scps.chat_part_id\n        ORDER BY m.date DESC\n        LIMIT 1\n    )\n    WHERE OLD.rowid = cp.chat_id\n    AND scps.ck_record_id IS NOT NULL;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS chat_part_service_on_insert_chat_part_message_join\nAFTER INSERT ON chat_part_message_join\nBEGIN\n    INSERT INTO chat_part_service (service, chat_part_id)\n    SELECT m.service, NEW.chat_part_id FROM message m\n    WHERE m.rowid = NEW.message_id\n    ON CONFLICT (service, chat_part_id) DO NOTHING;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS index_metrics_delete_propagation\nAFTER DELETE ON chat_part_message_join WHEN OLD.index_state != 2\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE index_state_metrics SET\n        pending_count = pending_count - CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n        donated_count = donated_count - CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n        redonation_count = redonation_count - CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END\n    WHERE id = 1;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS index_metrics_insert_propagation\nAFTER INSERT ON chat_part_message_join WHEN NEW.index_state != 2\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE index_state_metrics SET\n        pending_count = pending_count + CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n        donated_count = donated_count + CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,\n        redonation_count = redonation_count + CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END\n    WHERE id = 1;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS index_metrics_update_propagation\nAFTER UPDATE OF index_state ON chat_part_message_join\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE index_state_metrics SET\n        pending_count = pending_count +\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0) -\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0),\n        donated_count = donated_count +\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0) -\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0),\n        redonation_count = redonation_count +\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN NEW.index_state = 3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0) -\n            COALESCE(CASE WHEN OLD.index_state = 3 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END, 0)\n    WHERE id = 1;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS message_filter_action_update_propagation\nAFTER UPDATE OF filter_action, filter_sub_action ON message\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE chat_message_join SET filter_action = NEW.filter_action, filter_sub_action = NEW.filter_sub_action WHERE message_id = NEW.rowid;\nEND"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS message_filter_action_update_propagation\nAFTER UPDATE OF filter_action, filter_sub_action ON message\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE chat_part_message_join SET filter_action = NEW.filter_action, filter_sub_action = NEW.filter_sub_action WHERE message_id = NEW.rowid;\nEND"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS message_index_state_clear\nAFTER DELETE ON chat_part_message_join WHEN OLD.index_state = 1 OR OLD.index_state = 3\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE message SET index_state = 0 WHERE message.rowid = OLD.message_id;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS message_index_state_propagation\nAFTER UPDATE OF index_state ON message\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE chat_part_message_join SET index_state = NEW.index_state WHERE message_id = NEW.rowid;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS update_message_date_after_update_on_message\nAFTER UPDATE OF date ON message\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE chat_message_join SET message_date = NEW.date WHERE message_id = NEW.ROWID AND message_date != NEW.date;\nEND;"
+ "CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS update_message_date_after_update_on_message\nAFTER UPDATE OF date ON message\nBEGIN\n    UPDATE chat_part_message_join SET message_date = NEW.date WHERE message_id = NEW.ROWID AND message_date != NEW.date;\nEND;"
